     </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Savannah,_GA_City_Hall_IMG_4659.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="4608" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Savannah%2C_GA_City_Hall_IMG_4659.JPG/220px-Savannah%2C_GA_City_Hall_IMG_4659.JPG" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Savannah%2C_GA_City_Hall_IMG_4659.JPG/440px-Savannah%2C_GA_City_Hall_IMG_4659.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Savannah,_GA_City_Hall_IMG_4659.JPG" title="Ingrandisci">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         With its distinctive dome in tissue-paper-thin, 23-karat gold leaf, Savannah\'s City Hall (1906) is the first building constructed for exclusive use by the municipal government.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Oglethorpe_statue_in_Savannah,_GA_IMG_4716.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="4608" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Oglethorpe_statue_in_Savannah%2C_GA_IMG_4716.JPG/220px-Oglethorpe_statue_in_Savannah%2C_GA_IMG_4716.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Oglethorpe_statue_in_Savannah%2C_GA_IMG_4716.JPG/330px-Oglethorpe_statue_in_Savannah%2C_GA_IMG_4716.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Oglethorpe_statue_in_Savannah%2C_GA_IMG_4716.JPG/440px-Oglethorpe_statue_in_Savannah%2C_GA_IMG_4716.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Oglethorpe_statue_in_Savannah,_GA_IMG_4716.JPG" title="Ingrandisci">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Statue of\n         <a href="/wiki/James_Oglethorpe" title="James Oglethorpe">\n          James Oglethorpe\n         </a>\n         in Chippewa Square, completed in 1910 by\n         <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Chester_French" title="Daniel Chester French">\n          Daniel Chester French\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Savannah\n       </b>\n       (\n       <span class="nowrap">\n        <span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt">\n         <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">\n          /\n          <span style="border-bottom:1px dotted">\n           <span title="\'s\' in \'sigh\'">\n            s\n           </span>\n           <span title="/\xc9\x99/: \'a\' in \'about\'">\n            \xc9\x99\n           </span>\n           <span title="/\xcb\x88/: primary stress follows">\n            \xcb\x88\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'v\' in \'vie\'">\n            v\n           </span>\n           <span title="/\xc3\xa6/: \'a\' in \'bad\'">\n            \xc3\xa6\n           </span>\n           <span title="\'n\' in \'nigh\'">\n            n\n           </span>\n           <span title="/\xc9\x99/: \'a\' in \'about\'">\n            \xc9\x99\n           </span>\n          </span>\n          /\n         </a>\n        </span>\n       </span>\n       ) is the oldest city in the U.S. state of\n       <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(U.S._state)" title="Georgia (U.S. state)">\n        Georgia\n       </a>\n       and is the\n       <a href="/wiki/County_seat" title="County seat">\n        county seat\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/Chatham_County,_Georgia" title="Chatham County, Georgia">\n        Chatham County\n       </a>\n       . Established in 1733 on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Savannah_River" title="Savannah River">\n        Savannah River\n       </a>\n       , the city of Savannah became the\n       <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain">\n        British\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/British_America" title="British America">\n        colonial\n       </a>\n       capital of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Province_of_Georgia" title="Province of Georgia">\n        Province of Georgia\n       </a>\n       and later the first state capital of Georgia.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NewGA-Savannah_4-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NewGA-Savannah-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A strategic port city in the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Revolution" title="American Revolution">\n        American Revolution\n       </a>\n       and during the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Civil_War" title="American Civil War">\n        American Civil War\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Savannah is today an industrial center and an important Atlantic seaport. It is Georgia\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(U.S._state)#Major_cities" title="Georgia (U.S. state)">\n        fifth-largest city\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_metropolitan_areas_of_Georgia" title="List of metropolitan areas of Georgia">\n        third-largest metropolitan area\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Each year Savannah attracts millions of visitors to its cobblestone streets, parks, and notable historic buildings: the birthplace of\n       <a href="/wiki/Juliette_Gordon_Low" title="Juliette Gordon Low">\n        Juliette Gordon Low\n       </a>\n       (founder of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Girl_Scouts_of_the_USA" title="Girl Scouts of the USA">\n        Girl Scouts of the USA\n       </a>\n       ), the\n       <a href="/wiki/Georgia_Historical_Society" title="Georgia Historical Society">\n        Georgia Historical Society\n       </a>\n       (the oldest continually operating historical society in the South), the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Telfair_Museum_of_Art" title="Telfair Museum of Art">\n        Telfair Academy of Arts and Sciences\n       </a>\n       (one of the South\'s first public museums), the\n       <a href="/wiki/First_African_Baptist_Church_(Savannah,_Georgia)" title="First African Baptist Church (Savannah, Georgia)">\n        First African Baptist Church\n       </a>\n       (one of the oldest African-American Baptist congregations in the United States),\n       <a href="/wiki/Congregation_Mickve_Israel" title="Congregation Mickve Israel">\n        Temple Mickve Israel\n       </a>\n       (the third oldest synagogue in America), and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Central_of_Georgia_Railroad:_Savannah_Shops_and_Terminal_Facilities" title="Central of Georgia Railroad: Savannah Shops and Terminal Facilities">\n        Central of Georgia Railway roundhouse complex\n       </a>\n       (the oldest standing antebellum rail facility in America).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NewGA-Savannah_4-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NewGA-Savannah-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Savannah\'s downtown area, which includes the\n       <a href="/wiki/Savannah_Historic_District_(Savannah,_Georgia)" title="Savannah Historic District (Savannah, Georgia)">\n        Savannah Historic District\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Savannah_Victorian_Historic_District" title="Savannah Victorian Historic District">\n        Savannah Victorian Historic District\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Squares_of_Savannah,_Georgia" title="Squares of Savannah, Georgia">\n        22 parklike squares\n       </a>\n       , is one of the largest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Historic_Landmark_Districts" title="National Historic Landmark Districts">\n        National Historic Landmark Districts\n       </a>\n       in the United States (designated by the U.S. government in 1966).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NewGA-Savannah_4-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NewGA-Savannah-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-7">\n         [a]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Downtown Savannah largely retains the original town plan prescribed by founder\n       <a href="/wiki/James_Oglethorpe" title="James Oglethorpe">\n        James Oglethorpe\n       </a>\n       (a design now known as the\n       <a href="/wiki/Oglethorpe_Plan" title="Oglethorpe Plan">\n        Oglethorpe Plan\n       </a>\n       ). Savannah was the host city for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Sailing_at_the_1996_Summer_Olympics" title="Sailing at the 1996 Summer Olympics">\n        sailing competitions\n       </a>\n       during the\n       <a href="/wiki/1996_Summer_Olympics" title="1996 Summer Olympics">\n        1996 Summer Olympics\n       </a>\n       held in\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlanta" title="Atlanta">\n        Atlanta\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toc" id="toc">\n       <div class="toctitle">\n        <h2>\n         Contents\n        </h2>\n       </div>\n       <ul>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1">\n         <a href="#History">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           1\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n      <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Climate\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-4">\n           <a href="#Urban">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             2.2\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Urban\n            </span>\n           </a>\n           <ul>\n            <li class="toclevel-3 tocsection-5">\n             <a href="#Neighborhoods">\n              <span class="tocnumber">\n class="toctext">\n           Arts and culture\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-13">\n           <a href="#Books_and_literature">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             6.1\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Books and literature\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n Dance\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-15">\n           <a href="#Music">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             6.3\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Music\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-16">\n           <a        </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Squares\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-20">\n           <a           <a href="#Historic_cemeteries">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             7.4\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Historic cemeteries\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-23">\n           <a href="#Historic_forts">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             7.5\n            </span>\n            <span class="toctext">\n             Shopping\n            </span>\n           </a>\n          </li>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-26">\n           <a     </a>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-27">\n         <a href="#Sports_and_recreation">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           8\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Sports and recreation\n          </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-28">\n           <a </span>\n         </a>\n         <ul>\n          <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-34">\n           <a href="#Transportation">\n            <span class="tocnumber">\n             11.1\n cities\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-38">\n         <a href="#Unincorporated_suburbs_of_Savannah">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           14\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Unincorporated suburbs of Savannah\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1           Notes\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-41">\n         <a href="#References">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           17\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           References\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-42">\n         <a href="#Further_reading">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           18\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           Further reading\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-43">\n         <a href="#External_links">\n          <span class="tocnumber">\n           19\n          </span>\n          <span class="toctext">\n           External links\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="History">\n        History\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main articles:\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_Savannah,_Georgia" title="History of Savannah, Georgia">\n        History of Savannah, Georgia\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Timeline_of_Savannah,_Georgia" title="Timeline of Savannah, Georgia">\n        Timeline of Savannah, Georgia\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:JamesOlethrope.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1280" data-file-width="1159" height="188" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/JamesOlethrope.jpg/170px-JamesOlethrope.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/JamesOlethrope.jpg/255px-JamesOlethrope.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b7/JamesOlethrope.jpg/340px-JamesOlethrope.jpg 2x" width="170"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:JamesOlethrope.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/James_Oglethorpe" title="James Oglethorpe">\n          General James Edward Oglethorpe\n         </a>\n         , a philanthropist and a representative of\n         <a href="/wiki/George_II_of_Great_Britain" title="George II of Great Britain">\n          King George II\n         </a>\n         to the American colonies, was sent to create a buffer south of the\n         <a href="/wiki/Savannah_River" title="Savannah River">\n          Savannah River\n         </a>\n         to protect the Carolinas from Spanish Florida and French Louisiana.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On February 12, 1733,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/James_Oglethorpe" title="James Oglethorpe">\n        General James Oglethorpe\n       </a>\n       and settlers from the ship\n       <i>\n        Anne\n       </i>\n       landed at\n       <a href="/wiki/Yamacraw_Bluff" title="Yamacraw Bluff">\n        Yamacraw Bluff\n       </a>\n       and were greeted by\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tomo-Chi-Chi" title="Tomo-Chi-Chi">\n        Tomochichi\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Yamacraw" title="Yamacraw">\n        Yamacraws\n       </a>\n       , and Indian traders John and\n       <a href="/wiki/Mary_Musgrove" title="Mary Musgrove">\n        Mary Musgrove\n       </a>\n       . Mary Musgrove often served as an interpreter. The city of Savannah was founded on that date, along with the colony of Georgia. In 1751, Savannah and the rest of Georgia became a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Royal_Colony" title="Royal Colony">\n        Royal Colony\n       </a>\n       and Savannah was made the colonial capital of Georgia.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Savannah_9-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Savannah-9">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By the outbreak of the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Revolutionary_War" title="American Revolutionary War">\n        American Revolutionary War\n       </a>\n       , Savannah had become the southernmost commercial port of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Thirteen_Colonies" title="Thirteen Colonies">\n        Thirteen Colonies\n       </a>\n       . British troops took the city in 1778, and the following year a combined force of American and French soldiers failed to rout the British at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Siege_of_Savannah" title="Siege of Savannah">\n        Siege of Savannah\n       </a>\n       . The British did not leave the city until July 1782.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Savannah, a prosperous seaport throughout the nineteenth century, was the Confederacy\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Confederate_States_of_America#Demographics" title="Confederate States of America">\n        sixth most populous city\n       </a>\n       and the prime objective of General\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/William_T._Sherman" title="William T. Sherman">\n        William T. Sherman\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Sherman%27s_March_to_the_Sea" title="Sherman\'s March to the Sea">\n        March to the Sea\n       </a>\n       . Early on December 21, 1864, local authorities negotiated a peaceful surrender to save Savannah from destruction, and Union troops marched into the city at dawn.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-11">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Savannah was named for the Savannah River, which probably derives from variant names for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Shawnee" title="Shawnee">\n        Shawnee\n       </a>\n       , a Native American people who migrated to the river in the 1680s. The Shawnee destroyed another Native people, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Westo" title="Westo">\n        Westo\n       </a>\n       , and occupied their lands at the head of the Savannah River\'s navigation on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Seaboard_fall_line" title="Atlantic Seaboard fall line">\n        fall line\n       </a>\n       , near present-day\n       <a href="/wiki/Augusta,_Georgia" title="Augusta, Georgia">\n        Augusta\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       These Shawnee, whose Native name was\n       <i>\n        \xc5\xa0a\xc2\xb7wano\xc2\xb7ki\n       </i>\n       (literally, "southerners"),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">\n        <a href="#cite_note-13">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       were known by several local variants, including Shawano, Savano, Savana and Savannah.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">\n        <a href="#cite_note-14">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Another theory is that the name Savannah refers to the extensive marshlands surrounding the river for miles inland, and is derived from the English term "\n       <a href="/wiki/Savanna" title="Savanna">\n        savanna\n       </a>\n       ", a kind of tropical grassland, which was borrowed by the English from Spanish\n       <i>\n        sabana\n       </i>\n       and used in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Southern_Colonies" title="Southern Colonies">\n        Southern Colonies\n       </a>\n       . (The Spanish word comes from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" title="Ta\xc3\xadno language">\n        Taino\n       </a>\n       word\n       <i>\n        zabana\n       </i>\n       .)\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">\n        <a href="#cite_note-15">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Still other theories suggest that the name Savannah originates from\n       <a href="/wiki/Algonquian_languages" title="Algonquian languages">\n        Algonquian\n       </a>\n       terms meaning not only "southerners" but perhaps "salt".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">\n        <a href="#cite_note-16">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">\n        <a href="#cite_note-17">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">\n        Geography\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Geography">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Savannah lies on the Savannah River, approximately 20\xc2\xa0mi (32\xc2\xa0km) upriver from the Atlantic Ocean.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-18">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       According to the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Census_Bureau" title="United States Census Bureau">\n        United States Census Bureau\n       </a>\n       (2011), the city has a total area of 108.7 square miles (281.5\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ), of which 103.1 square miles (267.0\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ) is land and 5.6 square miles (15\xc2\xa0km\n       <sup>\n        2\n       </sup>\n       ) is water (5.15%). Savannah is the primary port on the Savannah River and the largest port in the state of Georgia. It is also located near the\n       <a href="/wiki/Intracoastal_Waterway" title="Intracoastal Waterway">\n        U.S. Intracoastal Waterway\n       </a>\n       . Georgia\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Ogeechee_River" title="Ogeechee River">\n        Ogeechee River\n       </a>\n       flows toward the Atlantic Ocean some 16 miles (26\xc2\xa0km) south of downtown Savannah, and forms the southern city limit.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Savannah is prone to flooding. Five canals and several pumping stations have been built to help reduce the effects: Fell Street Canal, Pipe Makers Canal, Kayton Canal, Springfield Canal and Casey Canal, the first four draining north into the Savannah River and the last, the Casey, draining south into the Vernon River.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Climate">\n        Climate\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Climate">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Savannah\'s climate is classified as\n       <a href="/wiki/Humid_subtropical_climate" title="Humid subtropical climate">\n        humid subtropical\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a href="/wiki/K%C3%B6ppen_climate_classification" title="K\xc3\xb6ppen climate classification">\n        K\xc3\xb6ppen\n       </a>\n       <i>\n        Cfa\n       </i>\n       ). In the Deep South, this is characterized by long and almost tropical summers and short, mild winters. Savannah records few days of freezing temperatures each year (and has rare snowfall). Due to its proximity to the Atlantic coast, Savannah rarely experiences temperatures as extreme as those in Georgia\'s interior. Nevertheless, the extreme temperatures have officially ranged from 105\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (41\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C), on July 20, 1986, down to 3\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (\xe2\x88\x9216\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C), on\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/January_1985_Arctic_outbreak" title="January 1985 Arctic outbreak">\n        January 21, 1985\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TWC_19-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TWC-19">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Seasonally, Savannah tends to have hot and humid summers with frequent (but brief) thunderstorms that develop in the warm and tropical air masses, which are common. Although summers in Savannah are frequently sunny, half of Savannah\'s annual precipitation falls during the months of June through September. Average dewpoints in summer range from 67.8\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (20\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C) to 71.6\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (22\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C). Winters in Savannah are mild and sunny with average daily high temperatures close to 60\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F (16\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C). November and December are the driest months recorded at Savannah\xe2\x80\x93Hilton Head International Airport. Each year, Savannah reports 24 days on average with low temperatures below freezing, though in some years fewer than 10 nights will fall below freezing. Although decades might pass between snowfall events, Savannah has experienced snow on rare occasions, most notably in December 1989, when up to 3.9 inches were recorded in one day in parts of the city.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NOAA_20-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NOAA-20">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-21">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Savannah is at risk for\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricanes" title="Hurricanes">\n        hurricanes\n       </a>\n       , particularly of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verde_hurricane" title="Cape Verde hurricane">\n        Cape Verde\n       </a>\n       type. Because of its location in the Georgia Bight (the arc of the Atlantic coastline in Georgia and northern Florida) as well as the tendency for hurricanes to re-curve up the coast, Savannah has a lower risk of hurricanes than some other coastal cities such as\n       <a href="/wiki/Charleston,_South_Carolina" title="Charleston, South Carolina">\n        Charleston, South Carolina\n       </a>\n       . Savannah was seldom affected by hurricanes during the 20th century, with one exception being\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_David" title="Hurricane David">\n        Hurricane David\n       </a>\n       in 1979. However, the historical record shows that the city was frequently affected during the second half of the 19th century. The most prominent of these storms was the\n       <a href="/wiki/1893_Sea_Islands_hurricane" title="1893 Sea Islands hurricane">\n        1893 Sea Islands hurricane\n       </a>\n       , which killed at least 2,000 people. (This estimate may be low, as deaths among the many impoverished rural\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/African-Americans" title="African-Americans">\n        African-Americans\n       </a>\n       living on Georgia\'s barrier islands may not have been reported.)\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable collapsible" style="width:90%; The Signal Service began observations in 1874, and the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Weather_Service" title="National Weather Service">\n        National Weather Service\n       </a>\n       has kept records of most data continually since then; since 1948,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Savannah-Hilton_Head_International_Airport" title="Savannah-Hilton Head International Airport">\n        Savannah-Hilton Head International Airport\n       </a>\n       has served as Savannah\'s official meteorological station. Annual records (dating back to 1950) from the airport\'s weather station are available on the web.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">\n        <a href="#cite_note-27">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Urban">\n        Urban\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Urban">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Neighborhoods">\n        Neighborhoods\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Neighborhoods">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Savannah_Neighborhoods.jpg">\n         <img alt="A map showing the existing City of Savannah neighborhoods." class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3264" data-file-width="4224" height="170" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Savannah_Neighborhoods.jpg/220px-Savannah_Neighborhoods.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Savannah_Neighborhoods.jpg/330px-Savannah_Neighborhoods.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/Savannah_Neighborhoods.jpg/440px-Savannah_Neighborhoods.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Savannah_Neighborhoods.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Map showing city of Savannah neighborhoods.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Savannah is a city of diverse neighborhoods. More than 100 distinct neighborhoods can be identified in six principal areas of the city: Downtown (Landmark Historic District and Victorian District), Midtown, Southside, Eastside, Westside, and Southwest/West Chatham (recently annexed suburban neighborhoods).\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Historic_districts">\n        Historic districts\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Historic districts">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Besides the Savannah Historic District, one of the nation\'s largest, four other historic districts have been formally demarcated:\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">\n        <a href="#cite_note-28">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        Victorian District\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Cuyler-Brownsville District\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Thomas Square Historic District\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Pin Point Historic District\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Demographics">\n        Demographics\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Demographics">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n      <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/1990_United_States_Census" title="1990 United States Census">\n           1990\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         137,560\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         \xe2\x88\x922.9%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="text-align:center">\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/2000_United_States_Census" title="2000 United States Census">\n           2000\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         131,510\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         \xe2\x88\x924.4%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="text-align:center">\n         <b>\n          <a href="/wiki/2010_United_States_Census" title="2010 United States Census">\n           2010\n          </a>\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         136,286\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         3.6%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td style="text-align:center">\n         <b>\n          Est. 2016\n         </b>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px;">\n         146,763\n        </td>\n        <td style="font-size:85%">\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-USCensusEst2016_1-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-USCensusEst2016-1">\n           [1]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n        <td style="padding-left:8px; text-align: center;">\n         7.7%\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4" style="border-top:1px solid black; font-size:85%; text-align:left">\n         <center>\n          U.S. Decennial Census\n          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DecennialCensus_29-0">\n           <a href="#cite_note-DecennialCensus-29">\n            [26]\n           </a>\n          </sup>\n         </center>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       According to the U.S. Census Bureau, Savannah\'s 2016 estimated population was 146,763, up from the official 2010 count of 136,286 residents.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Census Bureau\'s 2016 estimated population of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Savannah_Metropolitan_Statistical_Area" title="Savannah Metropolitan Statistical Area">\n        Savannah metropolitan area\n       </a>\n       , defined by the Census Bureau as\n       <a href="/wiki/Bryan_County,_Georgia" title="Bryan County, Georgia">\n        Bryan\n       </a>\n       , Chatham, and\n       <a href="/wiki/Effingham_County,_Georgia" title="Effingham County, Georgia">\n        Effingham\n       </a>\n       counties, was 384,024.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Between 2000 and 2010, Savannah\'s metro area had grown from 293,000 to 347,611, an increase of 18.6 percent.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">\n        <a href="#cite_note-32">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Savannah is also the largest principal city of the Savannah-Hinesville-Statesboro Combined Statistical Area, a larger trading area that includes the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Savannah,_GA_MSA" title="Savannah, GA MSA">\n        Savannah\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hinesville-Fort_Stewart_metropolitan_area" title="Hinesville-Fort Stewart metropolitan area">\n        Hinesville-Fort Stewart\n       </a>\n       metropolitan areas and (since 2012) the Statesboro Micropolitan Statistical Area. The 2016 estimated population of this area was 539,753, up from 495,745 at the 2010 Census.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Savannah_(5559843151).png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3009" data-file-width="3009" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Savannah_%285559843151%29.png/220px-Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Savannah_%285559843151%29.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Savannah_%285559843151%29.png/330px-Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Savannah_%285559843151%29.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Savannah_%285559843151%29.png/440px-Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Savannah_%285559843151%29.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Race_and_ethnicity_2010-_Savannah_(5559843151).png" title="Ingrandisci">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Racial distribution map of Savannah and Chatham County (\n         <i>\n          source\n         </i>\n         : 2010 U.S. Census). Each dot represents 25 residents:\n         <span style="color:#ff0000">\n          <b>\n           white\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         ,\n         <span style="color:#0000ff">\n          <b>\n           black\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         ,\n         <span style="color:#00ff80">\n          <b>\n           Asian\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         ,\n         <span style="color:#ff8000">\n          <b>\n           Hispanic\n          </b>\n         </span>\n         or\n         <b>\n          other\n         </b>\n         (yellow).\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       In the official 2010\n       <a href="/wiki/Census" title="Census">\n        census\n       </a>\n       of Savannah, there were 136,286 people, 52,615 households, and 31,390 families residing in the city.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-census_34-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-census-34">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Population_density" title="Population density">\n        population density\n       </a>\n       was 1,759.5 people per square mile (679.4/km\xc2\xb2). There were 57,437 housing units at an average density of 768.5 per square mile (296.7/km\xc2\xb2). The racial makeup of the city was 55.04%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Black_(U.S._Census)" title="Black (U.S. Census)">\n        Black\n       </a>\n       , 38.03%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/White_(U.S._Census)" title="White (U.S. Census)">\n        White\n       </a>\n       , 2.00%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_(U.S._Census)" title="Asian (U.S. Census)">\n        Asian\n       </a>\n       , 0.03%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Native_American_(U.S._Census)" title="Native American (U.S. Census)">\n        Native American\n       </a>\n       , 0.01%\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific_Islander_(U.S._Census)" title="Pacific Islander (U.S. Census)">\n        Pacific Islander\n       </a>\n       , 0.93% from\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Race_(United_States_Census)" title="Race (United States Census)">\n        other races\n       </a>\n       , and 2.01% from two or more races.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hispanic_(U.S._Census)" title="Hispanic (U.S. Census)">\n        Hispanic\n       </a>\n       or\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Latino_(U.S._Census)" title="Latino (U.S. Census)">\n        Latino\n       </a>\n       of any race were 4.07% of the population.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Non-Hispanic_Whites" title="Non-Hispanic Whites">\n        Non-Hispanic Whites\n       </a>\n       were 32.6% of the population in 2010,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-census_34-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-census-34">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       compared to 46.2% in 1990.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">\n        <a href="#cite_note-35">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       There were 51,375 households out of which 28.5% had children under the age of 18 living with them, 35.2% were\n       <a href="/wiki/Marriage" title="Marriage">\n        married couples\n       </a>\n       living together, 21.7% had a female householder with no husband present, and 38.9% were non-families. 31.4% of all households were made up of individuals and 11.5% had someone living alone who was 65 years of age or older. The average household size was 2.45 and the average family size was 3.13.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In the city, the age distribution was as follows: 25.6% were under the age of 18, 13.2% from 18 to 24, 28.5% from 25 to 44, 19.5% from 45 to 64, and 13.3% who were 65 years of age or older. The median age was 32 years. For every 100 females there were 89.3 males. For every 100 females age 18 and over, there were 84.6 males.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The median income for a household in the city was $29,038, and the median income for a family was $36,410. Males had a median income of $28,545 versus $22,309 for females. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Per_capita_income" title="Per capita income">\n        per capita income\n       </a>\n       for the city was $16,921. About 17.7% of families and 21.8% of the population were below the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Poverty_line" title="Poverty line">\n        poverty line\n       </a>\n       , including 31.4% of those under age 18 and 15.1% of those age 65 or over.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Government">\n        Government\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Government">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Savannah,_Georgia,_US_City_Hall.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="6000" data-file-width="4000" height="330" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Savannah%2C_Georgia%2C_US_City_Hall.JPG/220px-Savannah%2C_Georgia%2C_US_City_Hall.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Savannah%2C_Georgia%2C_US_City_Hall.JPG/330px-Savannah%2C_Georgia%2C_US_City_Hall.JPG 1.5x, class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Savannah,_Georgia,_US_City_Hall.JPG" title="Ingrandisci">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A different view of City Hall\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Savannah_Aldermanic_Districts.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3264" data-file-width="4224" height="170" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Savannah_Aldermanic_Districts.jpg/220px-Savannah_Aldermanic_Districts.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Savannah_Aldermanic_Districts.jpg/330px-Savannah_Aldermanic_Districts.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5e/Savannah_Aldermanic_Districts.jpg/440px-Savannah_Aldermanic_Districts.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Savannah_Aldermanic_Districts.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Map displaying the Aldermanic districts of Savannah.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Savannah adopted a\n       <a href="/wiki/Council%E2%80%93manager_government" title="Council\xe2\x80\x93manager government">\n        council-manager\n       </a>\n       form of government in 1954. The city council consists of the mayor and eight aldermen, six of whom are elected from one of six aldermanic districts, with each district electing one member. The other two members and the mayor are elected at-large.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The council levies taxes, enacts ordinances, adopts the annual budget, and appoints the City Manager.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CityGov_36-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CityGov-36">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The City Manager enacts the policies and programs established by council, recommends an annual budget and work programs, appoints bureau and department heads, and exercises general supervision and control over all employees of the city.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CityGov_36-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CityGov-36">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="Police,_fire_department,_and_Savannah-Chatham_consolidation">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Police.2C_fire_department.2C_and_Savannah-Chatham_consolidation">\n        Police, fire department, and Savannah-Chatham consolidation\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Police, fire department, and Savannah-Chatham consolidation">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       In 2003 Savannah and Chatham County voted to merge their city and county\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Police_department" title="Police department">\n        police departments\n       </a>\n       . The\n       <a href="/wiki/Savannah-Chatham_Metropolitan_Police_Department" title="Savannah-Chatham Metropolitan Police Department">\n        Savannah-Chatham Metropolitan Police Department\n       </a>\n       was established on January 1, 2005, after the Savannah Police Department and Chatham County Police Department merged. The department has a number of specialty units, including: K-9, SWAT, Bomb Squad, Marine Patrol, Dive, Air Support and Mounted Patrol. The 9-1-1 Communications Dispatch Center handles all 9-1-1 calls for service within the county and city, including fire and EMS. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Savannah_(Georgia)_Fire_Department" title="Savannah (Georgia) Fire Department">\n        Savannah Fire Department\n       </a>\n       only serves the City of Savannah and remains separate from the other municipal firefighting organizations in Chatham County.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       While some\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Words_to_watch#Unsupported_attributions" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Words to watch">\n          <span title="The material near this tag possibly uses too-vague attribution or weasel words. (January 2014)">\n           who?\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       see the police merger as a step toward city-county\n       <a href="/wiki/Consolidated_city-county" title="Consolidated city-county">\n        consolidation\n       </a>\n       , Savannah is actually one of eight incorporated cities or towns in Chatham County. (The others are\n       <a href="/wiki/Bloomingdale,_Georgia" title="Bloomingdale, Georgia">\n        Bloomingdale\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Garden_City,_Georgia" title="Garden City, Georgia">\n        Garden City\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Pooler,_Georgia" title="Pooler, Georgia">\n        Pooler\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Wentworth,_Georgia" title="Port Wentworth, Georgia">\n        Port Wentworth\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Thunderbolt,_Georgia" title="Thunderbolt, Georgia">\n        Thunderbolt\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Tybee_Island,_Georgia" title="Tybee Island, Georgia">\n        Tybee Island\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Vernonburg,_Georgia" title="Vernonburg, Georgia">\n        Vernonburg\n       </a>\n       ). Although these seven smaller localities would remain independent from a consolidated government, they have long opposed any efforts to adopt a city-county merger. One fear is that consolidation would reduce county funding to areas outside of Savannah.\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">\n          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2014)">\n           citation needed\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="State_representation">\n        State representation\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: State representation">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Georgia_Department_of_Corrections" title="Georgia Department of Corrections">\n        Georgia Department of Corrections\n       </a>\n       operates the\n       <a href="/wiki/Coastal_State_Prison" title="Coastal State Prison">\n        Coastal State Prison\n       </a>\n       in Savannah.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">\n        <a href="#cite_note-37">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">\n        <a href="#cite_note-38">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">\n        Economy\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Economy">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <div style="width:52px">\n          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg">\n           <img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" height="39"        <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          This section\n          <b>\n           needs additional citations for\n           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability"   <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Eugene_Talmadge_Memorial_Bridge.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1001" data-file-width="1500" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/Eugene_Talmadge_Memorial_Bridge.jpg/220px-Eugene_Talmadge_Memorial_Bridge.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/Eugene_Talmadge_Memorial_Bridge.jpg/330px-Eugene_Talmadge_Memorial_Bridge.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/66/Eugene_Talmadge_Memorial_Bridge.jpg/440px-Eugene_Talmadge_Memorial_Bridge.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Eugene_Talmadge_Memorial_Bridge.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A container ship leaves the\n         <a href="/wiki/Port_of_Savannah" title="Port of Savannah">\n          Port of Savannah\n         </a>\n         after passing under the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eugene_Talmadge_Memorial_Bridge" title="Eugene Talmadge Memorial Bridge">\n          Talmadge Memorial Bridge\n         </a>\n         and proceeding down the Savannah River past the\n         <a href="/wiki/Savannah_Historic_District_(Savannah,_Georgia)" title="Savannah Historic District (Savannah, Georgia)">\n          Savannah Historic District\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Agriculture was essential to Savannah\'s economy during its first two centuries.\n       <a href="/wiki/Silk" title="Silk">\n        Silk\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indigo_plant" title="Indigo plant">\n        indigo\n       </a>\n       production, both in demand in England, were early export commodities. By 1767, almost a ton of silk per year was exported to England.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">\n        <a href="#cite_note-39">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Georgia\'s mild\n       <a href="/wiki/Climate" title="Climate">\n        climate\n       </a>\n       offered perfect conditions for growing\n       <a href="/wiki/Cotton" title="Cotton">\n        cotton\n       </a>\n       , which became the dominant commodity after the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Revolution" title="American Revolution">\n        American Revolution\n       </a>\n       . Its production under the\n       <a href="/wiki/Peculiar_institution" title="Peculiar institution">\n        plantation system\n       </a>\n       and shipment through the\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_of_Savannah" title="Port of Savannah">\n        Port of Savannah\n       </a>\n       helped the city\'s European immigrants to achieve wealth and prosperity.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In the nineteenth century, the Port of Savannah became one of the most active in the United States, and Savannahians had the opportunity to consume some of the world\'s finest goods, imported by foreign merchants. Savannah\'s port has always been a mainstay of the city\'s economy. In the early years of the United States, goods produced in the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_World" title="New World">\n        New World\n       </a>\n       had to pass through Atlantic ports such as Savannah\'s before they could be shipped to England.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Between 1912 and 1968, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Savannah_Machine_%26_Foundry" title="Savannah Machine &amp; Foundry">\n        Savannah Machine &amp; Foundry\n       </a>\n       Company was a shipbuilder in Savannah.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bloome_40-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Bloome-40">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The Port of Savannah, manufacturing, the military, and\n       <a href="/wiki/Tourism" title="Tourism">\n        tourism\n       </a>\n       have become Savannah\'s four major economic drivers in the twenty-first century. In 2006, the Savannah Area Convention &amp; Visitors Bureau reported over 6.85 million visitors to the city during the year. By 2011, the Bureau reported that the number of visitors the city attracted increased to 12.1 million. Lodging, dining, entertainment, and visitor-related transportation account for over $2 billion in visitors\' spending per year and employ over 17,000.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       For years, Savannah was the home of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Union_Camp" title="Union Camp">\n        Union Camp\n       </a>\n       , which housed the world\'s largest paper mill. The plant is now owned by\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Paper" title="International Paper">\n        International Paper\n       </a>\n       , and it remains one of Savannah\'s largest employers. Savannah is also home to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulfstream_Aerospace" title="Gulfstream Aerospace">\n        Gulfstream Aerospace\n       </a>\n       company, maker of private jets, as well as various other large industrial interests.\n       <a href="/wiki/TitleMax" title="TitleMax">\n        TitleMax\n       </a>\n       is headquartered in Savannah.\n       <a href="/wiki/Morris_Multimedia" title="Morris Multimedia">\n        Morris Multimedia\n       </a>\n       , a newspaper and television company, is also based in Savannah.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 2000,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/J._C._Bamford" title="J. C. Bamford">\n        JCB\n       </a>\n       , the third largest producer of construction equipment in the world and the leading manufacturer of backhoes and telescopic handlers, built its North American headquarters in Chatham County near Savannah in\n       <a href="/wiki/Pooler,_Georgia" title="Pooler, Georgia">\n        Pooler\n       </a>\n       on I-95 near Savannah-Hilton Head International Airport.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In 2009-2014, Savannah was North America\'s fourth largest port for shipping container traffic.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Arts_and_culture">\n        Arts and culture\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Arts and culture">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Primary_sources" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <div style="width:52px">\n          <a class="image"        <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          This section\n          <b>\n           relies too much on\n           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">\n            references\n           </a>\n           to\n           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:No_original_research#Primary.2C_secondary_and_tertiary_sources" title="Wikipedia:No original research">\n href="/wiki/Wikipedia:No_original_research#Primary.2C_secondary_and_tertiary_sources" title="Wikipedia:No original research">\n            secondary or tertiary sources\n           </a>\n           .\n          </span>\n          <small>\n           <i>\n            (June 2009)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n          <small class="hide-when-compact">\n           <i>\n            (\n            <a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">\n             Learn how and when to remove this template message\n            </a>\n            )\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Beyond its architectural significance as being the nation\'s largest, historically restored urban area, the city of Savannah has a rich and growing performing arts scene, offering cultural events throughout the year.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Books_and_literature">\n        Books and literature\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Books and literature">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        The Savannah Book Festival \xe2\x80\x93 an annual book fair held on Presidents\' Day weekend in the vicinity of historic Telfair and Wright squares, includes free presentations by more than 35 contemporary authors. Special events with featured writers are offered at nominal cost throughout the year.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n         <a href="#cite_note-42">\n          [39]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Flannery_O%27Connor_Childhood_Home" title="Flannery O\'Connor Childhood Home">\n         Flannery O\'Connor Childhood Home\n        </a>\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">\n         <a href="#cite_note-43">\n          [40]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 a museum house dedicated to the work and life of the acclaimed fiction writer\n        <a href="/wiki/Flannery_O%27Connor" title="Flannery O\'Connor">\n         Flannery O\'Connor\n        </a>\n        , who was born in Savannah. In addition to its museum, the house offers literary programming, including the annual Ursrey Lecture honoring American fiction writers.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">\n         <a href="#cite_note-44">\n          [41]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Dance">\n        Dance\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Dance">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Savannah Ballet Theatre\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 established in 1998 as a nonprofit organization, it has grown to become the city\'s largest dance company.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45">\n        <a href="#cite_note-45">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Music">\n        Music\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Music">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Savannah_GA_USA_Lucas_Theater.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="4000" data-file-width="6000" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Savannah_GA_USA_Lucas_Theater.JPG/220px-Savannah_GA_USA_Lucas_Theater.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Savannah_GA_USA_Lucas_Theater.JPG/330px-Savannah_GA_USA_Lucas_Theater.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Savannah_GA_USA_Lucas_Theater.JPG/440px-Savannah_GA_USA_Lucas_Theater.JPG 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Savannah_GA_USA_Lucas_Theater.JPG" title="Ingrandisci">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Lucas Theatre for the Arts\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        The Coastal Jazz Association\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 presents a variety of jazz performances throughout the year in addition to hosting the annual Savannah Jazz Festival.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">\n         <a href="#cite_note-46">\n          [43]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Savannah Children\'s Choir\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 non-profit, auditioned choir for children in 2nd through 8th grades that performs throughout the community and in annual holiday and spring concerts.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">\n         <a href="#cite_note-47">\n          [44]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Savannah Concert Association\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 presents a variety of guest artists for chamber music performances each season. Performances are generally held in the Lucas Theatre For The Arts.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">\n         <a href="#cite_note-48">\n          [45]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/Savannah_Music_Festival" title="Savannah Music Festival">\n         Savannah Music Festival\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 an annual music festival of diverse artists which is Georgia\'s largest musical arts festival and is nationally recognized as one of the best music festivals in the world.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The Savannah Orchestra\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 Savannah\'s professional orchestra, which presents an annual season of classical and popular concert performances.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">\n         <a href="#cite_note-49">\n          [46]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The Savannah Philharmonic\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 professional orchestral and choral organization presenting year round concerts (classical, pops, education).\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">\n         <a href="#cite_note-50">\n          [47]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The Savannah Winds\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 amateur concert band hosted by the music department of Armstrong State University.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">\n         <a href="#cite_note-51">\n          [48]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The Armstrong Youth Orchestra\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 Savannah\'s professional orchestra for elementary, middle school, high school and some college students.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52">\n         <a href="#cite_note-52">\n          [49]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Theater_and_performance">\n        Theater and performance\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Theater and performance">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        Muse Arts Warehouse\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 founded in 2010, Muse Arts Warehouse is a nonprofit organization committed to community-building through the arts by providing a venue that is available, affordable, and accessible to Savannah\'s individual artists, arts organizations and the public.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53">\n         <a href="#cite_note-53">\n          [50]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Savannah Children\'s Theatre\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 a non-profit, year-round drama theater company geared toward offering elementary through high school students (and adults) opportunities for participation in dramatic and musical productions.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54">\n         <a href="#cite_note-54">\n          [51]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Savannah Community Theatre\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 a full theater season with a diverse programming schedule, featuring some of Savannah\'s finest actors in an intimate, three-quarter-round space.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">\n         <a href="#cite_note-55">\n          [52]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Little Theatre of Savannah\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 founded in 1950, The Little Theatre of Savannah, Inc., is a nonprofit, volunteer-based community organization dedicated to the celebration of the theater arts. Recognizing the unique social value, expressive fulfillment and opportunity for personal growth that theater provides its participants, the Little Theatre of Savannah invites all members of the community to participate both on- and off-stage.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56">\n         <a href="#cite_note-56">\n          [53]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        <a href="/wiki/The_Savannah_Theatre" title="The Savannah Theatre">\n         The Savannah Theatre\n        </a>\n        \xe2\x80\x93 Savannah\'s only fully professional resident theater, producing music revues with live singers, dancers and the most rockin\' band in town. Performances happen year-round, with several different titles and a holiday show.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57">\n         <a href="#cite_note-57">\n          [54]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Lucas Theatre for the Arts\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 founded in December 1921, the Lucas Theatre is one of several theaters owned by the Savannah College of Art and Design. It hosts the annual Savannah Film Festival.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Trustees Theater\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 once known as the Weis Theater, which opened February 14, 1946, this theater reopened as the Trustees Theater on May 9, 1998, and hosts a variety of performances and concerts sponsored by the Savannah College of Art and Design. SCAD also owns the building.\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        Odd Lot Improv\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 founded in 2010, a family-friendly improv comedy troupe performing weekly shows on Mondays and Fridays.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58">\n         <a href="#cite_note-58">\n          [55]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        House of Gunt \xe2\x80\x93 alternative drag collective founded in 2013 with monthly shows at Club One on top of other performances around the city throughout the year.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59">\n         <a href="#cite_note-59">\n          [56]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Visual_and_community_arts">\n        Visual and community arts\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Visual and community arts">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        Art Rise Savannah, Inc. \xe2\x80\x93 a local community nonprofit devoted to increasing access to the arts and improving opportunities for artists in the city.\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60">\n         <a href="#cite_note-60">\n          [57]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Points_of_interest">\n        Points of interest\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Savannah,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Points of interest">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Confederate_Memorial;_Savannah,_Georgia.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="450" height="227" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/98/Confederate_Memorial%3B_Savannah%2C_Georgia.jpg/170px-Confederate_Memorial%3B_Savannah%2C_Georgia.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/98/Confederate_Memorial%3B_Savannah%2C_Georgia.jpg/255px-Confederate_Memorial%3B_Savannah%2C_Georgia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/98/Confederate_Memorial%3B_Savannah%2C_Georgia.jpg/340px-Confederate_Memorial%3B_Savannah%2C_Georgia.jpg 2x" width="170"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Confederate_Memorial;_Savannah,_Georgia.jpg" title="Ingrandisci">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Confederate Memorial in\n         <a href="/wiki/Forsyth_Park" title="Forsyth Park">\n          Forsyth Park\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:German_Memorial_Fountain_in_Savannah,_Georgia_IMG_4714.JPG">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3456" data-file-width="4608" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/German_Memorial_Fountain_in_Savannah%2C_Georgia_IMG_4714.JPG/220px-German_Memorial_Fountain_in_Savannah%2C_Georgia_IMG_4714.JPG"
